			<div class="entry-content-wrapper clearfix">
                <header class="entry-content-header"></header><div class="entry-content"  itemprop="text" ><p>Students in the Biomedical Research Minor work on real research projects that are potentially publishable. As of December 2023, there are 532 publications in peer-reviewed journals with one or more of our students or alumni as co-authors. For a list of student authors, click <a href="https://www.biomedresearchminor.ucla.edu/minor-in-biomedical-research-student-publications/minor-in-biomedical-research-student-authors/">here</a>.</p>
